# FORGE Football (American) Coach Review Sample Pack

**Generated**: 2026-06-23  
**Generator**: `scripts/generate_coach_review_samples.py`  
**Purpose**: External S&C coach review — 36 samples across 6 roles × 3 levels

## How to Use This Pack

1. Review the **Coverage Matrix** below to understand the scope.
2. Each **role × level** section contains two samples (A and B).
3. Each sample includes: athlete profile, rationale, full program, exposure summary.
4. At the end of each sample, use the **Coach Review Prompts** to guide your feedback.
5. Record your overall feedback in the separate **Review Sheet** (`*_review_sheet.md`).

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: goalkeeper
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

### Coach Review Prompts

- [ ] Does this **Goalkeeper (Beginner)** program feel role-appropriate?
- [ ] Is the weekly training frequency appropriate for this athlete archetype?
- [ ] Are exercise selections and sequencing coach-like and sport-relevant?
- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

## Sample: FOOTBALL_GOALKEEPER_BEGINNER_B

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_GOALKEEPER_BEGINNER_B` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Goalkeeper |
| **Level** | Beginner |
| **Age** | 17 |
| **Training Age** | 0.8 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 2 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Basic Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.7 |
| **Strength Base Met** | No |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.4
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Low

### Program Summary

| Metric | Value |
|---|---|
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Duration** | 8 weeks |
| **Frequency** | 3x/week |
| **Conditioning Emphasis** | Pre Season — Strength |
| **Competition Window** | Off-season |
| **Role Emphasis** | goalkeeper — football |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
football Athlete (strength)
Blueprint: Full Body Strength | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Basic Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (100%)

Personalization:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

 Wk | Intent             | Tests                          | Adj | Notes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
W 1 | accumulation       | Jump / Power, Movement / Techn |     | 
W 2 | accumulation       |                                |     | 
W 3 | intensification    |                                |     | 
W 4 | intensification    |                                |     | 
W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |     | 
W 6 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |     | 
W 7 | taper              |                                |     | 
W 8 | deload             |                                |     | 

Exposure by Week:
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 1 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        Low  | Jump/Landing: High
    Deceleration:  Low  | Rotation:     Low
    Conditioning:  Low

Role Week Bias:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role

  Lower conditioning density than role baseline

  Rotation exposure target: Low

Testing / Benchmarking:

  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test

============================================================
```

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Acc] Acc
    - Band Pull-Apart  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPush] HPush
    - Wall Push-Up  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: Long Slow Distance — Base Builder
    Continuous running at conversational pace (able to speak in full sentences)
  Est. time: 40 min
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: strength | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: goalkeeper
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Days/Week** | 3 |

| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5

-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Low

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: goalkeeper
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

- [ ] Does this **Goalkeeper (Intermediate)** program feel role-appropriate?

- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?

| **Role** | Goalkeeper |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 22 |
| **Training Age** | 2.5 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.4
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4

-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Low

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: strength | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: goalkeeper
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Goalkeeper — Advanced

## Sample: FOOTBALL_GOALKEEPER_ADVANCED_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_GOALKEEPER_ADVANCED_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Goalkeeper |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.4
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.7
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Low
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: High
-   Deceleration exposure target: Low
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Low

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 30 |
| **Training Age** | 7.0 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | In Season |
| **Equipment** | Elite Facility |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Goalkeeper** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- Sprint exposure moderated per role
- Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Lower conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
  Sprint exposure moderated per role
  Jump/landing volume elevated per role
  Deceleration accumulation capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Lower conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Goalkeeper role -> jump-landing emphasis bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration accumulation capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

- Represents a **beginner Centre Back** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.7
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Moderate
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Program Summary

| Metric | Value |
|---|---|
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Duration** | 8 weeks |
| **Frequency** | 3x/week |
| **Conditioning Emphasis** | Pre Season — Power |
| **Competition Window** | Off-season |
| **Role Emphasis** | centre_back — football |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
football Athlete (power)
Blueprint: Full Body Strength | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (100%)

Personalization:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

W 7 | taper              |                                |     |
```

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPush] HPush
    - Wall Push-Up  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [VPush] VPush
    - Band Overhead Press  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: 20m Sprints
    20m maximal sprint.
  Est. time: 40 min

  [VPush] VPush
    - Band Overhead Press  2 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  1-2 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Est. time: 30 min

RECOVERY
------------------------------
  L1: Mobility + stretch (L1) — 10 min
  - General mobility flow (10 min)

==================================================
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: centre_back
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Centre Back** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: strength | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: centre_back
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?

| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 22 |
| **Training Age** | 2.5 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Centre Back** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.7
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Moderate
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role
- **Personalization**: Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: centre_back
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Centre Back — Advanced

## Sample: FOOTBALL_CENTRE_BACK_ADVANCED_A

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

| **Role** | Centre Back |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Strength |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Centre Back** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Strength** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.7
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.5
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   Moderate
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: Moderate
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (strength)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: strength | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (4 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Band YTWs (1 min)
      Cue: Squeeze shoulder blades, keep ribs down
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Sub-max bench (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Explosive concentric, controlled descent
    - Sub-max squat (50-60%) (1 min)
      Cue: Stand fast, controlled descent
```

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.

- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Role week note**: High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 30 |
| **Training Age** | 7.0 years |

| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | In Season |
| **Equipment** | Elite Facility |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Centre Back** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Centre Back role -> maximal force / collision robustness bias
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline
  High-eccentric tolerance allowed per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
football Athlete (speed)
Blueprint: Sprint Development | Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym

W 3 | intensification    |                                |     |

W 6 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 7 | taper              |                                |     | 
W 8 | deload             |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families

  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
```

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3 x 15-20m  |  technique focus  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Plyo] Plyo
    - Pogo Jump  2-3 x 4-6  |  quality, 2-3s reset, conservative lower-complexity plyo  |  rest: 90s
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  2-3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season, in_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Sprint Development (ID: 10)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: fullback
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.7
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: fullback
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Credibility Score** | 0.96 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season, in_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Sprint Development (ID: 10)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: fullback
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4

-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

- Represents a **advanced Fullback** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

```
W 4 | intensification    |                                |     | 
W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |     |

W 7 | taper              |                                |     |

Exposure by Week:
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 1 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 1 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 0 spd 0 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        High  | Jump/Landing: Low
    Deceleration:  High  | Rotation:     Low
    Conditioning:  High

Role Week Bias:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

Role Weekly Emphasis Targets:
  Force emphasis:           0.5
  Velocity emphasis:        0.7
  Conditioning emphasis:    0.7
  Rotation emphasis:        0.3
  Landing emphasis:         0.4
  Upper-body emphasis:      0.4

  Sprint exposure target:   High
  Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
  Deceleration exposure target: High
  Rotation exposure target: Low
  Conditioning density:     High

Testing / Benchmarking:
  Week 1: Movement / Technical Benchmark, Jump / Power Test
  Week 5: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 8: Lower Body Strength Test, Upper Body Strength Test, Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test, Conditioning Benchmark
```

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Fullback role -> velocity / speed-power / repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```

- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role

- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline

- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role

| **Equipment** | Basic Gym |

| **Strength Base Met** | No |
| **Blueprint** | Youth Foundation (U14-U20) |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

    - Air Squat  2 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - Glute Bridge  1-2 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [HPush] HPush
    - Wall Push-Up  2 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Scapular Retraction  1-2 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  1-2 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: 20m MAS Shuttle — Beginner Entry
    20m shuttle at beginner MAS pace (determined by 200m time-trial or estimated as 70-75% of max 20m sprint). Target: 5-6s per shuttle.
  Est. time: 40 min

RECOVERY
------------------------------
  L1: Mobility + stretch (L1) — 10 min
  - General mobility flow (10 min)

==================================================
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: midfielder
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.8
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4

-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps
```

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: midfielder
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Midfielder — Intermediate

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Midfielder |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 20 |
| **Training Age** | 2.0 years |
| **Goal** | Conditioning |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.8
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
```
