### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: midfielder
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

- [ ] Does this **Midfielder (Intermediate)** program feel role-appropriate?

- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

## Sample: FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_INTERMEDIATE_B

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_INTERMEDIATE_B` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Midfielder |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 22 |
| **Training Age** | 2.5 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.8
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: midfielder
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Midfielder — Advanced

## Sample: FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_ADVANCED_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_ADVANCED_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Midfielder |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Conditioning |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Strength + Conditioning |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.8
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-5 x 20-40m  |  max velocity or accel  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: MAS 60m Standard
    60m in target time (determined by MAS test: distance covered in 60s all-out = MAS pace per 60m). Typically 8-10s per 60m.
  Est. time: 40 min

--- W1 S2 (accumulation) ---

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Role week note**: Higher conditioning density than role baseline
- **Personalization**: Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Advanced
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: midfielder
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions
- **Validation**: {'type': 'info', 'message': 'Check volume load match: needs attention'}

- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

## Sample: FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_ADVANCED_B

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_MIDFIELDER_ADVANCED_B` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Midfielder |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 30 |
| **Training Age** | 7.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | In Season |
| **Equipment** | Elite Facility |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Midfielder** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role
- Higher conditioning density than role baseline

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.6
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.8
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     High

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Midfielder role -> repeat conditioning bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role
  Higher conditioning density than role baseline

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role

| **Level** | Beginner |

| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Basic Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.7 |
| **Strength Base Met** | No |
| **Blueprint** | Youth Foundation (U14-U20) |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Winger** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Velocity emphasis:        0.8
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4

-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: winger
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Winger** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Velocity emphasis:        0.8
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3 x 15-20m  |  technique focus  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Air Squat  3 x 8-12  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 3:00 min

    - Glute Bridge  2-3 x 10-15  |  pain-free, quality  |  rest: 45s

    - Plank  2-3 x 20-30s holds / 8-12 reps  |  quality, brace  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: 20m MAS Shuttle — Beginner Entry

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: winger
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Level** | Intermediate |

| **Training Age** | 2.0 years |
| **Goal** | Speed |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Strength + Power |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.89 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Winger** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Velocity emphasis:        0.8
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
-

-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 4x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_POWER — Hybrid strength-power development. Heavy strength + explosive work in same session.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Power (ID: 2)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: winger
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 4x/week — 32 total sessions

| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 22 |
| **Training Age** | 2.5 years |

| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Strength + Conditioning |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Winger** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Conditioning** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.3
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.8
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-4 x 20-30m  |  build to max  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min
  [HPush] HPush
    - Barbell Bench Press  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  3 x 8-10  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 90s
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  3 x 30-45s holds / 10-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  Conditioning: MAS 60m Standard
    60m in target time (determined by MAS test: distance covered in 60s all-out = MAS pace per 60m). Typically 8-10s per 60m.
  Est. time: 40 min

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.STRENGTH_CONDITIONING — Strength maintenance + energy system development. Common in pre-season / GPP blocks.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season | **Best training age**: 1-4 years
- **Role week note**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Strength + Conditioning (ID: 3)
- **Rationale**: Goal: conditioning | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: winger
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

### Coach Review Prompts

- [ ] Does this **Winger (Intermediate)** program feel role-appropriate?
- [ ] Is the weekly training frequency appropriate for this athlete archetype?
- [ ] Are exercise selections and sequencing coach-like and sport-relevant?
- [ ] Does the conditioning density match the sport's physiological demands?
- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

# Winger — Advanced

## Sample: FOOTBALL_WINGER_ADVANCED_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_WINGER_ADVANCED_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Winger |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Speed |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Sprint Development |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.96 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Winger** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Jump/landing volume capped per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.3
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.8
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.3
-   Landing emphasis:         0.4
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.4
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Low
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
football Athlete (speed)
Blueprint: Sprint Development | Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym
Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (96%)

Personalization:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

 Wk | Intent             | Tests                          | Adj | Notes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
W 1 | accumulation       | Jump / Power, Movement / Techn |     | 
W 2 | accumulation       |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 3 | intensification    |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 4 | intensification    |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 5 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 6 | realization        | Jump / Power, Sprint / Speed   |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 7 | taper              |                                |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families
W 8 | test               | Conditioning Benchmark, Lower  |   Y | Prev week high impact; reduced families

Exposure by Week:
  W1 (accumulation        ): 18 ex | 3 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W2 (accumulation        ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W3 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W4 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 1 rot
  W5 (intensification     ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 1 rot
  W6 (peak                ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W7 (taper               ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot
  W8 (deload              ): 15 ex | 0 sqt 3 hng 3 spd 3 lnd 0 rot

  Role Exposure Targets:
    Sprint:        High  | Jump/Landing: Low
    Deceleration:  High  | Rotation:     Low
    Conditioning:  Moderate

Role Week Bias:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias

Testing / Benchmarking:
  Week 1: Movement / Technical Benchmark, Jump / Power Test
  Week 5: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test
  Week 6: Jump / Power Test, Sprint / Speed Test

============================================================

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

  [TEST] Lower Body Strength Test | Upper Body Strength Test | Jump / Power Test | Sprint / Speed Test | Conditioning Benchmark
  [Sprint] Sprint
    - Acceleration Wall Drill  3-4 x 20-40m  |  max velocity or accel  |  rest: 3:00 min
  [Plyo] Plyo
    - Squat Jump  3-4 x 3-5  |  max intent, reactive  |  rest: 2:30 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  2-3 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPull] HPull
    - Dumbbell Row  2-3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-8  |  rest: 2:00 min
  [Core] Core
    - Plank  2-3 x 45-60s holds / 12-15 reps  |  quality, anti-movement  |  rest: 45s
  [Adj] Prev week high impact; reduced families
  Est. time: 25 min

RECOVERY
------------------------------
  L1: Mobility + stretch (L1) — 10 min
  - General mobility flow (10 min)

==================================================
```

- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (conditioning)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: conditioning | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Jump/landing volume capped per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Winger role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Jump/landing volume capped per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role

# Striker — Beginner

## Sample: FOOTBALL_STRIKER_BEGINNER_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_STRIKER_BEGINNER_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Striker |
| **Level** | Beginner |
| **Age** | 16 |
| **Training Age** | 0.5 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 2 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Basic Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.7 |
| **Strength Base Met** | No |
| **Blueprint** | Youth Foundation (U14-U20) |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.5 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.5
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 2x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.YOUTH_FOUNDATION — Build movement literacy, general strength, and athleticism. No specialisation. Fun + competence.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season, in_season, transition | **Best training age**: 0-2 years
- **Role week note**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Youth Foundation (U14-U20) (ID: 7)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: striker
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 2x/week — 16 total sessions

- [ ] Is the loading / intensity progression realistic for this level?
- [ ] What is the single most impactful change you would make?
- [ ] Would you trust this program with a real athlete at this level?

| **Blueprint** | Sprint Development |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.96 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **beginner Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 0.8 year(s) with limited gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Basic Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.5
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5

-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Beginner | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Basic Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

  [DLKD] DLKD

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season, in_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Sprint Development (ID: 10)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Beginner
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: striker
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Striker — Intermediate

## Sample: FOOTBALL_STRIKER_INTERMEDIATE_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_STRIKER_INTERMEDIATE_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Striker |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 20 |
| **Training Age** | 2.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Off Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.0 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Off Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.5
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test

    - RDL  3 x 6-8  |  RPE 7-9  |  rest: 4:00 min

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: striker
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

| **Role** | Striker |
| **Level** | Intermediate |
| **Age** | 22 |
| **Training Age** | 2.5 years |
| **Goal** | Speed |
| **Days/Week** | 3 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.85 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Sprint Development |
| **Credibility Score** | 0.96 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **intermediate Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 2.5 year(s) with solid gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Intermediate | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.SPRINT_DEVELOPMENT — Max velocity and/or acceleration improvement. Strength underpins but speed is priority.
- **Best phase**: pre_season, off_season, in_season | **Best training age**: 2-5 years
- **Role week note**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Sprint Development (ID: 10)
- **Rationale**: Goal: speed | Level: Intermediate
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: striker
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

# Striker — Advanced

## Sample: FOOTBALL_STRIKER_ADVANCED_A

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_STRIKER_ADVANCED_A` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Striker |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 26 |
| **Training Age** | 5.0 years |
| **Goal** | Power |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 60 min |
| **Season Phase** | Pre Season |
| **Equipment** | Commercial Gym |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 5.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Power** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **Pre Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Commercial Gym** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **A** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.5
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (power)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: power | Equipment: Commercial Gym

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - Leg swings (front/back) (1 min)
      Cue: Swing from hip, not lower back
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Pass-through (PVC) (0 min)
      Cue: Keep arms straight, go overhead and back
  Potentiate (2 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Box jump (build-up) (1 min)
      Cue: Land soft, stick each rep
    - Band-resisted sprint starts (1 min)
      Cue: Drive hard for 5 steps

--- W1 S1 (accumulation) ---
  [TEST] Movement / Technical Benchmark | Jump / Power Test
  [DLKD] DLKD
    - Goblet Squat  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [DLHD] DLHD
    - RDL  3-4 x 3-5  |  RPE 8-9  |  rest: 5:00 min
  [HPush] HPush

### Program Rationale

- **Blueprint**: BlueprintName.FULL_BODY_STRENGTH — General strength accrual across all major movement patterns. Highest frequency of each pattern per week.
- **Best phase**: off_season, pre_season | **Best training age**: 0-3 years
- **Role week note**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Role week note**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Role week note**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Personalization**: Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- **Personalization**: Sprint exposure elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- **Personalization**: Rotational exposure moderated per role
- **Rationale**: Blueprint: Full Body Strength (ID: 1)
- **Rationale**: Goal: power | Level: Advanced
- **Rationale**: Role-aware planning applied: striker
- **Rationale**: Block: 8 weeks, 3x/week — 24 total sessions

### Athlete Profile

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Sample ID** | `FOOTBALL_STRIKER_ADVANCED_B` |
| **Sport** | Football (American) |
| **Role** | Striker |
| **Level** | Advanced |
| **Age** | 30 |
| **Training Age** | 7.0 years |
| **Goal** | Speed |
| **Days/Week** | 4 |
| **Session Duration** | 75 min |
| **Season Phase** | In Season |
| **Equipment** | Elite Facility |
| **Technique Consistency** | 0.95 |
| **Strength Base Met** | Yes |
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Why This Sample Exists

- Represents a **advanced Striker** athlete in the **football (american)** pathway.
- Training age of 7.0 year(s) with extensive gym history.
- Goal emphasis: **Speed** — drives blueprint selection and session architecture.
- Competition context: **In Season** — affects volume, intensity, and conditioning density.
- Equipment access: **Elite Facility** — constrains exercise selection and loading options.
- Variant **B** of two — differs in goal emphasis, training load, or seasonal context to show FORGE's range within the same archetype.

### Role Profile / Bias Summary

- Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
- Sprint exposure elevated per role
- Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
- Rotational exposure moderated per role

-   Force emphasis:           0.5
-   Velocity emphasis:        0.7
-   Conditioning emphasis:    0.6
-   Rotation emphasis:        0.4
-   Landing emphasis:         0.5
-   Upper-body emphasis:      0.5
- 
-   Sprint exposure target:   High
-   Jump/Landing exposure target: Moderate
-   Deceleration exposure target: High
-   Rotation exposure target: Low
-   Conditioning density:     Moderate

### Program Summary

| Metric | Value |
|---|---|
| **Blueprint** | Full Body Strength |
| **Duration** | 8 weeks |
| **Frequency** | 3x/week |
| **Conditioning Emphasis** | In Season — Speed |
| **Competition Window** | Off-season |
| **Role Emphasis** | striker — football |
| **Credibility Score** | 1.0 |

### Block Overview (Week-by-Week)

```
BLOCK SUMMARY
============================================================
football Athlete (speed)

Program Score: 1.0/1.0 (100%)

  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

### Full Program Output

```
football Athlete (speed)
==================================================
Level: Advanced | 3x/week | 8 weeks
Goal: speed | Equipment: Elite Facility

Personalization Notes:
  Striker role -> velocity / speed-power bias
  Sprint exposure elevated per role
  Deceleration emphasis elevated per role
  Rotational exposure moderated per role

WARMUP
------------------------------
  Raise (3 min)
    - Forward jog (2 min)
      Cue: Light feet, tall posture
    - Skipping (basic) (1 min)
      Cue: Soft feet, quick ground contact
  Activate (3 min)
    - World's greatest stretch (1 min)
      Cue: Open chest to ceiling, back knee off ground
    - Glute bridge (double) (0 min)
      Cue: Squeeze glutes at top, 2s hold
    - Dead bug (0 min)
      Cue: Press low back into floor, move opposite limbs
    - Cossack squat (1 min)
      Cue: Shift weight fully to bent leg, keep heel down
  Potentiate (1 min)
    - Pogo jumps (0 min)
      Cue: Minimal knee bend, stiff ankles, quick ground contact
    - Build-up sprint (60-80%) (1 min)
      Cue: Progressive acceleration, tall posture
